###
Supplementary Data 3. Predicted secondary structure (pKiss) for library variants with systematic sequence alterations in the region
downstream of the slippery site.
The first line of each record (starting with ">") denotes the library ID (see Supplementary Data 2 for information about and readouts 
for the respective variants).
The second line contains the primary (DNA) sequence of the region downstream of the slippery site.
The third line contains the MFE as calculated using pKiss and the corresponding predicted secondary structure (including two classes
of pseudoknots).
###
